## גֵּא (id: 001235000000000)

גֵּא
====

גֵּא (H1341)

adj · גאה

Great 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ גָּאֹון · גַּאֲוָה · עֶבְרָה

proud, arrogant \= state in which humans have an elevated status in their own eyes, ≈ which is seen as a negative and undesirable attitude for humans

[ISA 16:6](https://ref.ly/Isa16:6)

Matthew P. Anstey

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 16:6


## גאה (id: 001236000000000)

גאה
===

גאה (H1342)

verb · גֵּא · גֵּאָה · גֵּאֶה · גַּאֲוָה · גָּאֹון · גֵּאוּת · גַּאֲיֹון · גֵּוָה · גְּאוּאֵל

High 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ שׂגה

to grow, to become tall, to become high, to rise \= process by which plants and other inanimate objects increase in height

[JOB 8:11](https://ref.ly/Job8:11) · [EZK 47:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek47:5)

Stance 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to raise oneself up \= action by which humans raises themselves up or lift up part of their body; ≈ associated with pride

[JOB 10:16](https://ref.ly/Job10:16)1

Great 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to show (one's) greatness \= action by which a deity shows his majesty and greatness ◄ by his actions, ► which is a reason for praise

[EXO 15:1](https://ref.ly/Exod15:1) · [EXO 15:1](https://ref.ly/Exod15:1) · [EXO 15:21](https://ref.ly/Exod15:21) · [EXO 15:21](https://ref.ly/Exod15:21)

1 JOB 10:16 MT HOTTP\-B (connects it to רֹאשׁ in previous verse) \| RSV NIV REB GNT CEV ואגאה \| NJB NRSV "proud/bold" \| NJPS "it is something to be proud of"

Matthew P. Anstey

* **Associated Passages:** Job 8:11; Ezekiel 47:5; Job 10:16; Exodus 15:1; Exodus 15:21

|  |
| --- |

 ≠ שָׁפֵל

proud, arrogant \= state in which humans have an elevated status in their own eyes, ≈ which is seen as a negative and undesirable attitude for humans

[JOB 40:11](https://ref.ly/Job40:11) · [JOB 40:12](https://ref.ly/Job40:12) · [PSA 94:2](https://ref.ly/Ps94:2) · [PSA 140:6](https://ref.ly/Ps140:6) · [PRO 15:25](https://ref.ly/Prov15:25) · [PRO 16:19](https://ref.ly/Prov16:19) · [ISA 2:12](https://ref.ly/Isa2:12) · [JER 48:29](https://ref.ly/Jer48:29)

## גַּאֲוָה (id: 001240000000000)

גַּאֲוָה
========

גַּאֲוָה (H1346)

noun f · גאה

High

rising, swelling \= state in which a substance increases in volume, which manifests itself in an increasing height

[PSA 46:4](https://ref.ly/Ps46:4)1

Great 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ בּוּז · גָּאֹון · גֵּא · גֹּבַהּ · גֹּדֶל לֵבָב · עֶבְרָה · עֹז · עֵזֶר · עָתָק · רֻם לֵב 

|  |
| --- |

 ≠ שְׁפַל־רוּחַ

greatness, glory, pride, arrogance \= state in which humans or deities have an elevated status, either in their own eyes or in the eyes of other people, ≈ which can either be good or bad, depending on whether this status is justified

[DEU 33:26](https://ref.ly/Deut33:26) · [DEU 33:29](https://ref.ly/Deut33:29) · [JOB 41:7](https://ref.ly/Job41:7)3 · [PSA 10:2](https://ref.ly/Ps10:2) · [PSA 31:19](https://ref.ly/Ps31:19) · [PSA 31:24](https://ref.ly/Ps31:24) · [PSA 36:12](https://ref.ly/Ps36:12) · [PSA 46:4](https://ref.ly/Ps46:4)1 · [PSA 68:35](https://ref.ly/Ps68:35) · [PSA 73:6](https://ref.ly/Ps73:6) · [PRO 14:3](https://ref.ly/Prov14:3)4 · [PRO 29:23](https://ref.ly/Prov29:23) · [ISA 9:8](https://ref.ly/Isa9:8) · [ISA 13:3](https://ref.ly/Isa13:3) · [ISA 13:11](https://ref.ly/Isa13:11) · [ISA 16:6](https://ref.ly/Isa16:6) · [ISA 25:11](https://ref.ly/Isa25:11) · [JER 48:29](https://ref.ly/Jer48:29) · [ZEP 3:11](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:11)

1 PSA 46:4 NIV "surging" NJPS "swell" NJB "heaves" ESV "swelling" \= \[1a] \| RSV NRSV "tumult" GNT "violence" \= \[1b]? \| REB his majesty" \= \[1c] \| Dahood "its midst" \= גֵּו 2 JOB 41:7 NEW NOTE 3 JOB 41:7 MT NJPS "pride" \| HOTTP\-C RSV NIV NRSV REB GNT CEV ESV "back" \= גַּו 4 PRO 14:3 MT HOTTP\-A LXX "ὕβρις" NJPS "haughtiness" NJB "pride" GNT CEV "proud" \| RSV NIV NRSV REB ESV "back" \= גֵּו

Matthew P. Anstey

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 46:4; Deuteronomy 33:26; Deuteronomy 33:29; Job 41:7; Psalms 10:2; Psalms 31:19; Psalms 31:24; Psalms 36:12; Psalms 68:35; Psalms 73:6; Proverbs 14:3; Proverbs 29:23; Isaiah 9:8; Isaiah 13:3; Isaiah 13:11; Isaiah 16:6; Isaiah 25:11; Jeremiah 48:29; Zephaniah 3:11


## גְּאוּלִים (id: 001241000000000)

גְּאוּלִים
==========

גְּאוּלִים (H1350b) [SAHD](https://sahd-online.com/words/g2ulim/)

noun m · גאל

Safe

redemption, deliverance \= causative action by which a deity delivers an individual or group of people from the power of someone else or from difficult circumstances, ► which usually implies that the one who performed the act of deliverance has the right to claim the ones he delivered for himself

[ISA 63:4](https://ref.ly/Isa63:4)

A. Gray

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 63:4


## גָּאֹון (id: 001242000000000)

גָּאֹון
=======

גָּאֹון (H1347)

noun m · גאה

Landscapes 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ עֵץ · יַעַר · חֹרֶשׁ · סְבַךְ

thicket \= dense growth of shrubbery or small trees, habitat of animals

[JER 12:5](https://ref.ly/Jer12:5) · [JER 49:19](https://ref.ly/Jer49:19) · [JER 50:44](https://ref.ly/Jer50:44) · [ZEC 11:3](https://ref.ly/Zech11:3)

noun m · גאה

Great 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ גֵּא · גֵּאֶה · גַּאֲוָה · גֹּבַהּ · גֹּבַהּ רוּחַ · הָדָר · הֹוד · עֶבְרָה · רֻם לֵב · תִּפְאֶרֶת

greatness, glory, majesty, pride, arrogance \= state in which humans or deities have an elevated status, either in their own eyes or in the eyes of other people, ≈ which can either be good or bad, depending on whether this status is justified

## גֵּאוּת (id: 001243000000000)

גֵּאוּת
=======

גֵּאוּת (H1348)

noun f · גאה

High

rising, swelling \= state in which a substance increases in volume, which manifests itself in an increasing height

[PSA 89:10](https://ref.ly/Ps89:10) · [ISA 9:17](https://ref.ly/Isa9:17)

Great

greatness, glory, majesty, pride, arrogance \= state in which humans or deities have an elevated status, either in their own eyes or in the eyes of other people, ≈ which can either be good or bad, depending on whether this status is justified

[PSA 17:10](https://ref.ly/Ps17:10) · [PSA 93:1](https://ref.ly/Ps93:1) · [ISA 12:5](https://ref.ly/Isa12:5) · [ISA 26:10](https://ref.ly/Isa26:10) · [ISA 28:1](https://ref.ly/Isa28:1) · [ISA 28:3](https://ref.ly/Isa28:3)

Matthew P. Anstey

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 89:10; Isaiah 9:17; Psalms 17:10; Psalms 93:1; Isaiah 12:5; Isaiah 26:10; Isaiah 28:1; Isaiah 28:3

## גאל (id: 001245000000000)

גאל
===

גאל (H1350a · H1351) — גֹּאֵל [SAHD](https://sahd-online.com/words/g-2-l/)

verb · גְּאוּלִים · גְּאֻלָּה

Free 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

to redeem oneself, to reclaim oneself \= action by which humans who have been enslaved regain their freedom, which is normally achieved by paying a price

[LEV 25:49](https://ref.ly/Lev25:49)

Free 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb nif

to redeem, to reclaim \= causative action by which humans cause a person, animal, or inanimate object that has become someone else's property to be restored to its original state, which is normally achieved by paying a price

[LEV 25:25](https://ref.ly/Lev25:25) · [LEV 25:30](https://ref.ly/Lev25:30) · [LEV 25:33](https://ref.ly/Lev25:33) · [LEV 25:48](https://ref.ly/Lev25:48) · [LEV 25:49](https://ref.ly/Lev25:49) · [LEV 25:49](https://ref.ly/Lev25:49) · [LEV 25:54](https://ref.ly/Lev25:54) · [LEV 27:13](https://ref.ly/Lev27:13) · [LEV 27:13](https://ref.ly/Lev27:13) · [LEV 27:15](https://ref.ly/Lev27:15) · [LEV 27:19](https://ref.ly/Lev27:19) · [LEV 27:19](https://ref.ly/Lev27:19) · [LEV 27:20](https://ref.ly/Lev27:20) · [LEV 27:20](https://ref.ly/Lev27:20) · [LEV 27:27](https://ref.ly/Lev27:27) · [LEV 27:28](https://ref.ly/Lev27:28) · [LEV 27:31](https://ref.ly/Lev27:31) · [LEV 27:31](https://ref.ly/Lev27:31) · [LEV 27:33](https://ref.ly/Lev27:33) · [RUT 3:13](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:13) · [RUT 3:13](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:13) · [RUT 3:13](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:13) · [RUT 3:13](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:13) · [RUT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:4) · [RUT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:4) · [RUT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:4) · [RUT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:4) · [RUT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:4) · [RUT 4:6](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:6) · [RUT 4:6](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:6) · [RUT 4:6](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:6) · [JOB 3:5](https://ref.ly/Job3:5) · [ISA 52:3](https://ref.ly/Isa52:3)

People 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

kinship\-redeemer, to fulfil one's duty as kinsman, avenger \= a person with the duty to help close relatives regain possession of objects that used to be theirs but that have become someone else's property, which may include their own personal freedom; this person also has the responsibility to avenge the death of a relative, which can also be seen as an act of redemption

[LEV 25:25](https://ref.ly/Lev25:25) · [LEV 25:26](https://ref.ly/Lev25:26) · [NUM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Num5:8) · [NUM 35:12](https://ref.ly/Num35:12) · [NUM 35:19](https://ref.ly/Num35:19) · [NUM 35:21](https://ref.ly/Num35:21) · [NUM 35:24](https://ref.ly/Num35:24) · [NUM 35:25](https://ref.ly/Num35:25) · [NUM 35:27](https://ref.ly/Num35:27) · [NUM 35:27](https://ref.ly/Num35:27) · [DEU 19:6](https://ref.ly/Deut19:6) · [DEU 19:12](https://ref.ly/Deut19:12) · [JOS 20:3](https://ref.ly/Josh20:3) · [JOS 20:5](https://ref.ly/Josh20:5) · [JOS 20:9](https://ref.ly/Josh20:9) · [RUT 2:20](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:20) · [RUT 3:9](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:9) · [RUT 3:12](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:12) · [RUT 3:12](https://ref.ly/Ruth3:12) · [RUT 4:1](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:1) · [RUT 4:3](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:3) · [RUT 4:6](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:6) · [RUT 4:8](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:8) · [RUT 4:14](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:14) · [2SA 14:11](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:11) · [1KI 16:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs16:11)

Safe 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ ישׁע · נצל · פדה · קנה

to redeem, to deliver \= causative action by which humans or deity deliver an individual or group of people from the power of someone else or from difficult circumstances, ► which usually implies that the one who performed the act of deliverance has the right to claim the ones he delivered for himself

[GEN 48:16](https://ref.ly/Gen48:16) · [EXO 6:6](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6) · [EXO 15:13](https://ref.ly/Exod15:13) · [JOB 19:25](https://ref.ly/Job19:25) · [PSA 19:15](https://ref.ly/Ps19:15) · [PSA 69:19](https://ref.ly/Ps69:19) · [PSA 72:14](https://ref.ly/Ps72:14) · [PSA 74:2](https://ref.ly/Ps74:2) · [PSA 77:16](https://ref.ly/Ps77:16) · [PSA 78:35](https://ref.ly/Ps78:35) · [PSA 103:4](https://ref.ly/Ps103:4) · [PSA 106:10](https://ref.ly/Ps106:10) · [PSA 107:2](https://ref.ly/Ps107:2) · [PSA 107:2](https://ref.ly/Ps107:2) · [PSA 119:154](https://ref.ly/Ps119:154) · [PRO 23:11](https://ref.ly/Prov23:11) · [ISA 35:9](https://ref.ly/Isa35:9) · [ISA 41:14](https://ref.ly/Isa41:14) · [ISA 43:1](https://ref.ly/Isa43:1) · [ISA 43:14](https://ref.ly/Isa43:14) · [ISA 44:6](https://ref.ly/Isa44:6) · [ISA 44:22](https://ref.ly/Isa44:22) · [ISA 44:23](https://ref.ly/Isa44:23) · [ISA 44:24](https://ref.ly/Isa44:24) · [ISA 47:4](https://ref.ly/Isa47:4) · [ISA 48:17](https://ref.ly/Isa48:17) · [ISA 48:20](https://ref.ly/Isa48:20) · [ISA 49:7](https://ref.ly/Isa49:7) · [ISA 49:26](https://ref.ly/Isa49:26) · [ISA 51:10](https://ref.ly/Isa51:10) · [ISA 52:9](https://ref.ly/Isa52:9) · [ISA 54:5](https://ref.ly/Isa54:5) · [ISA 54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:8) · [ISA 59:20](https://ref.ly/Isa59:20) · [ISA 60:16](https://ref.ly/Isa60:16) · [ISA 62:12](https://ref.ly/Isa62:12) · [ISA 63:9](https://ref.ly/Isa63:9) · [ISA 63:16](https://ref.ly/Isa63:16) · [JER 31:11](https://ref.ly/Jer31:11) · [JER 50:34](https://ref.ly/Jer50:34) · [LAM 3:58](https://ref.ly/Lam3:58) · [HOS 13:14](https://ref.ly/Hos13:14) · [MIC 4:10](https://ref.ly/Mic4:10)

verb · גֹּעַל

Unclean 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif, verb hit

to defile oneself \= action by which humans cause themselves to be physically contaminated ◄ by getting in direct contact with unclean objects, such as unclean food and blood

[ISA 59:3](https://ref.ly/Isa59:3) · [LAM 4:14](https://ref.ly/Lam4:14) · [DAN 1:8](https://ref.ly/Dan1:8) · [DAN 1:8](https://ref.ly/Dan1:8)

Unclean 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi, verb pu'al, verb hif

to stain, to pollute \= causative action by which humans cause an object to be physically contaminated ◄ by causing it to get in direct contact with dirt or other unclean objects

[ISA 63:3](https://ref.ly/Isa63:3) · [MAL 1:7](https://ref.ly/Mal1:7) · [MAL 1:7](https://ref.ly/Mal1:7)1 · [MAL 1:12](https://ref.ly/Mal1:12)

Evil 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ מרא

to defile oneself \= action by which humans cause themselves to be morally contaminated ◄ by their evil deeds

[ZEP 3:1](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:1)

Unwilling 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pu'al

to disqualify, to exclude, to reject literally: to treat as unclean; hence: \= action by which someone is declared unfit for a certain position or task

[EZR 2:62](https://ref.ly/Ezra2:62) · [NEH 7:64](https://ref.ly/Neh7:64)

noun m · גֹּוב · גֹּבַי

Swarming Creatures 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ חָסִיל

locust, grasshopper \= six\-legged, winged insect that is characterized by the fact that its third pair of legs is elongated and adapted to hopping; insects of this type move in swarms at certain periods and migrate to new areas, which they colonize; at other times they live either solitary or in small groups; ◄ Acrididae family; ► normally eaten cooked by toasting, grilling, frying, or broiling, though in some places they are also eaten raw; clean animal, that may be eaten; ≈ associated with destruction

[ISA 33:4](https://ref.ly/Isa33:4)

noun m

## גְּבוּלָה (id: 001258000000000)

גְּבוּלָה
=========

גְּבוּלָה (H1367)

noun f · גבל

Non\-Whole

boundary, territory \= a set of limits that separates part of a whole from other parts, with focus either on the limits itself or on the area or object surrounded by it

[NUM 32:33](https://ref.ly/Num32:33) · [NUM 34:2](https://ref.ly/Num34:2) · [NUM 34:12](https://ref.ly/Num34:12) · [DEU 32:8](https://ref.ly/Deut32:8) · [JOS 18:20](https://ref.ly/Josh18:20) · [JOS 19:49](https://ref.ly/Josh19:49) · [JOB 24:2](https://ref.ly/Job24:2) · [PSA 74:17](https://ref.ly/Ps74:17) · [ISA 10:13](https://ref.ly/Isa10:13) · [ISA 28:25](https://ref.ly/Isa28:25)

Enio R. Mueller

noun m · גבר

People

## גֹּבַי (id: 001264000000000)

גֹּבַי
======

גֹּבַי (H1462)

noun m · גֵּב

Swarming Creatures

locust \= six\-legged, winged insect that is characterized by the fact that its third pair of legs is elongated and adapted to hopping; insects of this type move in swarms at certain periods and migrate to new areas, which they colonize; at other times they live either solitary or in small groups; ◄ Acrididae family; ► normally eaten cooked by toasting, grilling, frying, or broiling, though in some places they are also eaten raw; clean animal, that may be eaten; ≈ associated with large quantities and destruction

[AMO 7:1](https://ref.ly/Amos7:1) · [NAM 3:17](https://ref.ly/Nah3:17)1

1 NAM 3:17 The phrase כְּגֹוב גֹּבָי "like a locust of locusts" is normally taken as a case of dittography from an original כְּגֹבָי "like locusts", as per LXX. Most versions translate it as a collective noun phrase: RSV "like clouds of locusts", NJPS "like piles of hoppers", NJB "like swarms of hoppers", NIV "like swarms of locusts". The Vulgate follows the MT more closely "quasi lucustae lucustarum", "like (the) locusts of locusts".

Matthew P. Anstey

* **Associated Passages:** Amos 7:1; Nahum 3:17

## גַּד (id: 001291000000000)

גַּד
====

גַּד (H1407 · H1408 · H1409)

noun m

Plants

coriander \= a plant of about 60 cm in height; its upper leaves are finely divided and its lower ones broad; it has tiny white or reddish flowers, and a strong odor; its seeds are oily, brown or gray, and about the size of small peas; ◄ Coriandrum sativum; ► its leaves and seeds used in cooking; fragrant oil from the seeds is sometimes used in making perfume and medicine; ≈ it is used to describe the appearance of manna

[EXO 16:31](https://ref.ly/Exod16:31) · [NUM 11:7](https://ref.ly/Num11:7)

name · גַּדִּיאֵל · גַּדִּי

Names of Deities

good fortune, luck \= an unpredictable and uncontrollable force that shapes events favorably; ≈ it may have religious connotations, in that the force is attributed to a god of good fortune

[GEN 30:11](https://ref.ly/Gen30:11) · [ISA 65:11](https://ref.ly/Isa65:11)2

1 GEN 30:11 MT\-K בגד \| MT\-Q בָּא גָד 2 ISA 65:11 There is disagreement as to whether the reference is to good fortune per se, or the name of a god: RSV NIV NRSV ESV "Fortune" NJPS "Luck" NJB "Gad" GNT "Gad ... the god of luck" CEV "Good Luck"

## גְּדוּד (id: 001297000000000)

גְּדוּד
=======

גְּדוּד (H1416 · H1417)

noun m · גדד

Groups 

|  |
| --- |

 Soldiers

band of raiders, troops \= a group of armed humans equipped for fighting on land, whose main purpose is to execute swift attacks and loot and plunder as much as they can; sometimes also used to denote a unit of a more regular army

[GEN 49:19](https://ref.ly/Gen49:19) · [1SA 30:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam30:8) · [1SA 30:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam30:15) · [1SA 30:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam30:15) · [1SA 30:23](https://ref.ly/1Sam30:23) · [2SA 3:22](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:22) · [2SA 4:2](https://ref.ly/2Sam4:2) · [2SA 22:30](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:30)1 · [1KI 11:24](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:24) · [2KI 5:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs5:2) · [2KI 6:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:23) · [2KI 13:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:20) · [2KI 13:21](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:21) · [2KI 24:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs24:2) · [2KI 24:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs24:2) · [2KI 24:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs24:2) · [2KI 24:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs24:2) · [1CH 7:4](https://ref.ly/1Chr7:4) · [1CH 12:19](https://ref.ly/1Chr12:19) · [1CH 12:22](https://ref.ly/1Chr12:22) · [2CH 22:1](https://ref.ly/2Chr22:1) · [2CH 25:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr25:9) · [2CH 25:10](https://ref.ly/2Chr25:10) · [2CH 25:13](https://ref.ly/2Chr25:13) · [2CH 26:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr26:11) · [JOB 19:12](https://ref.ly/Job19:12) · [JOB 25:3](https://ref.ly/Job25:3) · [JOB 29:25](https://ref.ly/Job29:25) · [PSA 18:30](https://ref.ly/Ps18:30)1 · [JER 18:22](https://ref.ly/Jer18:22) · [HOS 6:9](https://ref.ly/Hos6:9) · [HOS 7:1](https://ref.ly/Hos7:1) · [MIC 4:14](https://ref.ly/Mic4:14)2

noun m

Landforms

ridge, barrier, wall \= a raised strip of earth or other material

## גְּדוּדָה (id: 001298000000000)

גְּדוּדָה
=========

גְּדוּדָה (H1418)

noun f

Impact

gash \= wound, inflicted on oneself with a knife, ► as a sign of mourning

[JER 48:37](https://ref.ly/Jer48:37)

## גְּדוּלָּה (id: 001300000000000)

גְּדוּלָּה
==========

גְּדוּלָּה (H1420) — גְּדוּלָה

noun f · גדל

Great

greatness \= state in which a human being or deity has an elevated status, as a result of their authority, rank, wealth, or wisdom

Quantity

noun m

Tombs 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ קֶבֶר

tomb \= a place where dead people are buried

[JOB 21:32](https://ref.ly/Job21:32)1

1 JOB 21:32 · JOB 5:26 The close association with sheaves and death in "You will come to the grave in ripe old age, as shocks are taken away in their season", suggests that the meaning of \[2] may be related to \[1]. Similarly, DCH lists all four uses under one base meaning "shock (of grain)", saying that in Job 21:32 perhaps it is used collectively to mean burial mound.

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 22:5; Judges 15:5; Job 5:26; Job 21:32

## גדע (id: 001318000000000)

גדע
===

Detach 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

to break off \= process by which part of an object, without apparent human intervention, detaches itself from a larger unit, so that it falls to the ground

[ISA 22:25](https://ref.ly/Isa22:25)

Detach 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pi, verb nif, verb pu'al

to cut off, to cut down \= causative action by which part of an object is violently removed from a larger unit, with the help of a sharp object, so that it falls to the ground

stone fence, wall \= a continuous vertical structure, usually made of natural stones, that encloses or divides an area of land; ≈ associated with security; in some cases used figuratively to denote integrity, which can be negatively affected by sin

## גֹּוב (id: 001339000000000)

גֹּוב
=====

גֹּוב (H1359)

name

Names of Locations 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ גֶּזֶר‏

Gob \= town, possibly to be identified with Gezer; ► location where David fought the Philistines

[2SA 21:18](https://ref.ly/2Sam21:18) · [2SA 21:19](https://ref.ly/2Sam21:19)

noun m

Swarming Creatures

locust \= six\-legged, winged insect that is characterized by the fact that its third pair of legs is elongated and adapted to hopping; insects of this type move in swarms at certain periods and migrate to new areas, which they colonize; at other times they live either solitary or in small groups; ◄ Acrididae family; ► normally eaten cooked by toasting, grilling, frying, or broiling, though in some places they are also eaten raw; clean animal, that may be eaten; ≈ associated with large quantities

[NAM 3:17](https://ref.ly/Nah3:17)1 · [NAM 3:17](https://ref.ly/Nah3:17)1

1 NAM 3:17 · NAM 3:17 The phrase כְּגֹוב גֹּבָי "like a locust of locusts" is normally taken as a case of dittography from an original כְּגֹבָי "like locusts", as per LXX. Most versions translate it as a collective noun phrase: RSV "like clouds of locusts", NJPS "like piles of hoppers", NJB "like swarms of hoppers", NIV "like swarms of locusts". The Vulgate follows the MT more closely "quasi lucustae lucustarum", "like (the) locusts of locusts".

Matthew P. Anstey

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Samuel 21:18; 2 Samuel 21:19; Nahum 3:17

Groups

people, band literally: a nation; hence: \= a group of people pursuing a common goal

[2KI 6:18](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:18) · [PSA 43:1](https://ref.ly/Ps43:1) · [DAN 11:23](https://ref.ly/Dan11:23)

locust \= six\-legged, winged insect that is characterized by the fact that its third pair of legs is elongated and adapted to hopping; insects of this type move in swarms at certain periods and migrate to new areas, which they colonize; at other times they live either solitary or in small groups; ◄ Acrididae family; ► normally eaten cooked by toasting, grilling, frying, or broiling, though in some places they are also eaten raw; clean animal, that may be eaten

[JOL 1:4](https://ref.ly/Joel1:4) · [JOL 2:25](https://ref.ly/Joel2:25) · [AMO 4:9](https://ref.ly/Amos4:9)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Joel 1:4; Joel 2:25; Amos 4:9

Giloh \= town; ◄ located in the hill country; territory of Judah; ► home town of Ahitophel, counselor of David

## גִּלּוּל (id: 001417000000000)

גִּלּוּל
========

גִּלּוּל (H1544) — גִּלּוּלִים

noun m · גלל

Images 

|  |
| --- |

 Cult Objects 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אֱלִיל · חַמָּן · יִדְּעֹנִי · מִזְבֵּחַ · עָצָב · תְּרָפִים

image, idol \= a physical likeness or representation of a person, animal, or thing; ◄ usually made from stone or wood overlaid with gold or silver; ► functioning as an object of non\-sanctioned worship

Names of People

Gilead \= man; ► father of Jephthah, judge of Israel

[JDG 11:1](https://ref.ly/Judg11:1) · [JDG 11:2](https://ref.ly/Judg11:2)

Names of People

Gilead \= man; ◄ son of Michael; tribe of Gad

[1CH 5:14](https://ref.ly/1Chr5:14)

1 1KI 4:19 MT RSV NIV NJPS NRSV REB GNT CEV \| NJB Gad 2 HOS 6:8 Possibly a reference to one of the towns in Gilead, such as Adam (Andersen and Freedman, AYB) or Ramoth\-Gilead (Stuart, WBC).

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 26:29; Numbers 26:30; Numbers 27:1; Numbers 36:1; Joshua 17:3; Judges 5:17; 1 Chronicles 2:21; 1 Chronicles 2:23; 1 Chronicles 7:14; 1 Chronicles 7:17; Genesis 31:21; Genesis 31:23; Genesis 31:25; Genesis 37:25; Numbers 32:1; Numbers 32:26; Numbers 32:29; Numbers 32:39; Numbers 32:40; Deuteronomy 2:36; Deuteronomy 3:10; Deuteronomy 3:12; Deuteronomy 3:13; Deuteronomy 3:15; Deuteronomy 3:16; Deuteronomy 4:43; Deuteronomy 34:1; Joshua 12:2; Joshua 12:5; Joshua 13:11; Joshua 13:25; Joshua 13:31; Joshua 17:1; Joshua 17:5; Joshua 17:6; Joshua 20:8; Joshua 21:38; Joshua 22:9; Joshua 22:13; Joshua 22:15; Joshua 22:32; Judges 7:3; Judges 10:4; Judges 10:8; Judges 10:17; Judges 10:18; Judges 11:5; Judges 11:7; Judges 11:8; Judges 11:9; Judges 11:10; Judges 11:11; Judges 11:29; Judges 12:4; Judges 12:5; Judges 12:7; Judges 20:1; Judges 21:8; Judges 21:9; Judges 21:10; Judges 21:12; Judges 21:14; 1 Samuel 11:1; 1 Samuel 11:9; 1 Samuel 13:7; 1 Samuel 31:11; 2 Samuel 2:4; 2 Samuel 2:5; 2 Samuel 2:9; 2 Samuel 17:26; 2 Samuel 21:12; 2 Samuel 24:6; 1 Kings 4:13; 1 Kings 4:19; 1 Kings 17:1; 1 Kings 22:3; 1 Kings 22:4; 1 Kings 22:6; 1 Kings 22:12; 1 Kings 22:15; 1 Kings 22:20; 1 Kings 22:29; 2 Kings 8:28; 2 Kings 9:1; 2 Kings 9:4; 2 Kings 9:14; 2 Kings 10:33; 2 Kings 15:29; 1 Chronicles 2:22; 1 Chronicles 5:9; 1 Chronicles 5:10; 1 Chronicles 5:16; 1 Chronicles 6:65; 1 Chronicles 10:11; 1 Chronicles 26:31; 1 Chronicles 27:21; 2 Chronicles 18:2; 2 Chronicles 18:3; 2 Chronicles 18:5; 2 Chronicles 18:11; 2 Chronicles 18:14; 2 Chronicles 18:19; 2 Chronicles 18:28; 2 Chronicles 22:5; Psalms 60:9; Psalms 108:9; Song of Songs 4:1; Song of Songs 6:5; Jeremiah 8:22; Jeremiah 22:6; Jeremiah 46:11; Jeremiah 50:19; Ezekiel 47:18; Hosea 6:8; Hosea 12:12; Amos 1:3; Amos 1:13; Obadiah 1:19; Micah 7:14; Zechariah 10:10; Judges 11:1; Judges 11:2; 1 Chronicles 5:14


## גַּלְעֵד (id: 001436000000000)

גַּלְעֵד
========

גַּלְעֵד (H1567)

name · גַּל · עֵד

Names of Landforms

Galeed \= location ◄ east of the Jordan, (possibly in Gilead), ► where Jacob and Laban erected a pile of stones to commemorate their agreement

[GEN 31:47](https://ref.ly/Gen31:47) · [GEN 31:48](https://ref.ly/Gen31:48)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 31:47; Genesis 31:48


## גִּלְעָדִי (id: 001437000000000)

גִּלְעָדִי
==========

גִּלְעָדִי (H1569)

adj · גִּלְעָד

Names of Groups

Gileadite, from Gilead \= inhabitant or descendant of Gilead, tribe and territory of Manasseh

[NUM 26:29](https://ref.ly/Num26:29) · [JDG 10:3](https://ref.ly/Judg10:3) · [JDG 11:1](https://ref.ly/Judg11:1) · [JDG 11:40](https://ref.ly/Judg11:40) · [JDG 12:7](https://ref.ly/Judg12:7) · [2SA 17:27](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:27) · [2SA 19:32](https://ref.ly/2Sam19:32) · [1KI 2:7](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:7) · [2KI 15:25](https://ref.ly/2Kgs15:25) · [EZR 2:61](https://ref.ly/Ezra2:61) · [NEH 7:63](https://ref.ly/Neh7:63)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 26:29; Judges 10:3; Judges 11:1; Judges 11:40; Judges 12:7; 2 Samuel 17:27; 2 Samuel 19:32; 1 Kings 2:7; 2 Kings 15:25; Ezra 2:61; Nehemiah 7:63


## גלשׁ (id: 001438000000000)

גלשׁ
====

גלשׁ (H1570)

verb

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to descend, to surge down, to stream down exact meaning unsure; possibly: \= action by which animals move down from an elevated place by skipping down from one place to another, ≈ which produces an elegant picture

[SNG 4:1](https://ref.ly/Song4:1) · [SNG 6:5](https://ref.ly/Song6:5)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Song of Songs 4:1; Song of Songs 6:5

גַּם

גַּם (H1571)

adv

Extenders

 ≈ אַף

also, too, even, moreover, what is more, what is worse, furthermore, besides, and, both … and marker pointing to information that needs to be considered in addition to previous information (either explicit or implied)

Affirmers

indeed, yes, really? marker expressing a speaker's confirmation of the truth of a statement; in some cases the truth of this statement is conceded

[GEN 16:13](https://ref.ly/Gen16:13) · [GEN 20:6](https://ref.ly/Gen20:6) · [GEN 27:33](https://ref.ly/Gen27:33) · [GEN 44:10](https://ref.ly/Gen44:10) · [NUM 22:33](https://ref.ly/Num22:33) · [DEU 2:15](https://ref.ly/Deut2:15) · [1SA 24:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam24:12) · [2SA 17:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:16) · [2CH 20:4](https://ref.ly/2Chr20:4) · [NEH 3:35](https://ref.ly/Neh3:35) · [JOB 2:10](https://ref.ly/Job2:10) · [JOB 18:5](https://ref.ly/Job18:5) · [PSA 118:11](https://ref.ly/Ps118:11) · [PSA 119:24](https://ref.ly/Ps119:24) · [PSA 133:1](https://ref.ly/Ps133:1) · [ISA 13:3](https://ref.ly/Isa13:3) · [ISA 43:13](https://ref.ly/Isa43:13) · [JER 7:11](https://ref.ly/Jer7:11) · [HOS 9:12](https://ref.ly/Hos9:12) · [MAL 1:10](https://ref.ly/Mal1:10) · [MAL 2:2](https://ref.ly/Mal2:2)

Contrastors

yet marker pointing out that the information that follows is an unexpected consequence of what has been stated before

[LEV 26:44](https://ref.ly/Lev26:44) · [NEH 6:1](https://ref.ly/Neh6:1) · [PSA 129:2](https://ref.ly/Ps129:2) · [NAM 3:10](https://ref.ly/Nah3:10)

Perception

so, therefore \= marker pointing out that the information that follows represents the logical consequence of what has been stated before

## גָּמָל (id: 001449000000000)

גָּמָל
======

גָּמָל (H1581)

noun m

Domestic Animals

camel \= large quadruped mammal, which may reach a height of 2 m. or more; dromedaries are bigger and a uniform light fawn color; bactrians are darker; they are suited to life in desert areas, store excess food in their humps, can go without water for long periods, and can make long journeys through dry areas; ◄ Camelus dromedarius and Camelus bactrianus; ► they are used for riding and for carrying heavy loads and pulling carts; their hair is woven into cloth used for making tents or outer robes; their milk is used as food and drink; ≈ they are a symbol of wealth and commerce, but unclean and not to be eaten

## גנב (id: 001456000000000)

גנב
===

גנב (H1589)

verb · גַּנָּב · גְּנֵבָה

Possess 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pi, verb nif, verb pu'al

to steal \= action by which humans secretly take possession of objects belonging to someone else, and sometimes even of other humans, without permission or legal right and usually without intending to return it

Non\-Know 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

**Collocation:** גנב לֵב · גנב לֵבָב

to keep (someone) uninformed literally: \= to steal (someone's) heart; hence: \= action by which humans act in such a way that others are unaware

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb hit

to go secretly, to steal \= action by which humans move somewhere quietly or surreptitiously, like a thief who does not want to be seen

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pu'al

to bring secretly \= causative action by which someone causes someone else to move somewhere quietly or surreptitiously, like a thief who does not want to be seen

Constructions

winepress \= basin ◄ hewn out of a rock or lined with plaster ► into which harvested grapes were thrown and trampled to squeeze out the juice, which from there flowed into a trough or vat; ≈ treading a winepress is often used as a figure of speech to refer to God's anger and punishment
